template file?</a></li><li class="flex flex-row"><a href="#viewer-deudv" class="flex flex-row items-baseline left-[-1px] relative text-sm py-1 ps-3 hover:text-primary transition-all border-l border-transparent">Midway Summary</a></li><li class="flex flex-row"><a href="#viewer-e764c" class="flex flex-row items-baseline left-[-1px] relative text-sm py-1 ps-3 hover:text-primary transition-all border-l border-transparent">Gain stealthiness with GlobalDotName</a></li><li class="flex flex-row"><a href="#viewer-fr6tk" class="flex flex-row items-baseline left-[-1px] relative text-sm py-1 ps-3 hover:text-primary transition-all border-l border-transparent">Arming a template file with VBA</a></li><li class="flex flex-row"><a href="#viewer-eqedi" class="flex flex-row items-baseline left-[-1px] relative text-sm py-1 ps-3 hover:text-primary transition-all border-l border-transparent">Trust</a></li><li class="flex flex-row"><a href="#viewer-4aqju" class="flex flex-row items-baseline left-[-1px] relative text-sm py-1 ps-3 hover:text-primary transition-all border-l border-transparent">Setting up the persistence</a></li><li class="flex flex-row"><a href="#viewer-att0c" class="flex flex-row items-baseline left-[-1px] relative text-sm py-1 ps-3 hover:text-primary transition-all border-l border-transparent">Warning!</a></li><li class="flex flex-row"><a href="#viewer-804qh" class="flex flex-row items-baseline left-[-1px] relative text-sm py-1 ps-3 hover:text-primary transition-all border-l border-transparent">In The Wild</a></li><li class="flex flex-row"><a href="#viewer-bosma" class="flex flex-row items-baseline left-[-1px] relative text-sm py-1 ps-3 hover:text-primary transition-all border-l border-transparent">After words</a></li></ul><!--/$--><div class="flex flex-col gap-3 page-api-block:xl:max-2xl:px-3"><!--$--><div class="flex flex-col items-start gap-2 mt-2"><p class="text-sm text-dark/6 dark:text-light/5">Was this helpful?</p><div class="inline-flex items-center justify-center flex-row rounded-full straight-corners:rounded-sm ring-1 ring-inset ring-dark/2 h-8 dark:ring-light/1"><div page-api-block:xl:max-2xl:pr-0 page-api-block:max-w-[1654px] page-api-block:mx-auto"><header class="max-w-3xl mx-auto mb-6 space-y-3 page-api-block:ml-0"><h1 class="text-4xl font-bold flex items-center gap-4"><span class="emoji dark:text-light/6 text-inherit">🔍</span>Office Templates and GlobalDotName - A Stealthy Office Persistence Technique</h1></header><!--$--><div class="[&amp;&gt;*+*]:mt-5 grid whitespace-pre-wrap"><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">A few weeks back, I was researching various adversarial techniques, when a couple of minutes into the research of <a class="underline underline-offset-2 text-primary hover:text-primary-700 transition-colors " href="https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T1137/">T1137 </a>(Office Application Startup), there appeared to be a yet-to-be-documented capability that can be leveraged by adversaries using this technique.</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">I also noticed there isn&#x27;t a lot of in-depth information about some of the techniques presented in <a class="underline underline-offset-2 text-primary hover:text-primary-700 transition-colors " href="https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T1137/">T1137</a>, such a the &quot;Normal Template&quot; technique, even though plenty of well known threat actors like &quot;<a class="underline underline-offset-2 text-primary hover:text-primary-700 transition-colors " href="https://securityaffairs.co/wordpress/86953/apt/muddywater-powerstats-v3.html">MuddyWater</a>&quot; leverage this technique, so I decided to shed some light about it and some of Word&#x27;s inner workingarming a template file ws.</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">When researching adversarial techniques, I start by examining the <a class="underline underline-offset-2 text-primary hover:text-primary-700 transition-colors " href="https://attack.mitre.org/">MITRE ATT&amp;CK Post-Exploitation matrix</a> to check the technique&#x27;s existence, and gather additional information if exists on the web.</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">So at one point, I decided to research <a class="underline underline-offset-2 text-primary hover:text-primary-700 transition-colors " href="https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T1137/">T1137 </a>a.k.a &quot;Office Application Startup&quot;.</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><a class="underline underline-offset-2 text-primary hover:text-primary-700 transition-colors " href="https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T1137/">T1137 </a>documented multiple implementations for achieving persistence in Microsoft Office application startup such as &quot;Office Test&quot; key, Add-ins, Templates, Rules &amp; Home pages(Outlook), etc.</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">But today we&#x27;re here to talk about Office Templates; Office Templates will eventually allow us to execute code on each application startup, <strong class="font-bold">even on macro-free documents!</strong> (docx, pptx, etc).</p><h3 id="viewer-78dm0" class="text-2xl font-semibold group relative grid w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="grid grid-area-1-1 relative -ml-6 w-7 border-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-[0] group-focus:opacity-[0] md:group-hover:md:opacity-[1] md:group-focus:md:opacity-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><a href="#viewer-78dm0" aria-label="Direct link to heading" class="inline-flex h-full items-start dark:text-light/3 dark:shadow-none dark:ring-0 leading-snug"><svg style="mask-image:url(https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v6.6.0/svgs/regular/hashtag.svg?v=2&amp;token=a463935e93);mask-repeat:no-repeat;mask-position:center" class="gb-icon w-3.5 h-[1lh] transition-colors text-transparent group-hover:text-dark/6 dark:group-hover:text-light/5 lg:w-4"></svg></a></div><div class="grid-area-1-1 z-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><strong class="font-bold">How Does this Technique Work?</strong></div></h3><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">It&#x27;s relatively simple, every office application uses some form of a template, so if we will take Microsoft&#x27;s Office Word for example, When executed, it loads its &quot;<a class="underline underline-offset-2 text-primary hover:text-primary-700 transition-colors " href="https://support.office.com/en-us/article/change-the-normal-template-normal-dotm-06de294b-d216-47f6-ab77-ccb5166f98ea?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US">Normal Template</a>&quot; that contains default styles and customizations that determine the basic look of a document, and even active content such as macro.</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">By replacing the &quot;Normal Template&quot; of Word with an armed version of our own that contains VBA for example, we can achieve persistent code execution on the machine since the template will load each time a document is opened.</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">Later in this article, I will demonstrate how to arm your template, and how to make this technique even stealthier by using a custom template. We can define a custom template by using Word&#x27;s UI or by editing the registry value &quot;GlobalDotName&quot; which we will learn about shortly.</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">One extremely cool thing about this technique is that the armed template <strong class="font-bold">VBA code will be executed even when macro-free documents are executed!</strong> (.docx,pptx, etc)</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"></p><h3 id="viewer-c50r4" class="text-2xl font-semibold group relative grid w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="grid grid-area-1-1 relative -ml-6 w-7 border-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-[0] group-focus:opacity-[0] md:group-hover:md:opacity-[1] md:group-focus:md:opacity-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><a href="#viewer-c50r4" aria-label="Direct link to heading" class="inline-flex h-full items-start dark:text-light/3 dark:shadow-none dark:ring-0 leading-snug"><svg style="mask-image:url(https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v6.6.0/svgs/regular/hashtag.svg?v=2&amp;token=a463935e93);mask-repeat:no-repeat;mask-position:center" class="gb-icon w-3.5 h-[1lh] transition-colors text-transparent group-hover:text-dark/6 dark:group-hover:text-light/5 lg:w-4"></svg></a></div><div class="grid-area-1-1 z-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><strong class="font-bold">What is a template file?</strong></div></h3><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">All Microsoft Office applications use templates, but for the sake of this article, we&#x27;ll focus on Microsoft&#x27;s Office Word. Word&#x27;s default template file is named Normal.dot / Normal.dotm; it&#x27;s also been referred to as &quot;Normal Template&quot;.</p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"></p><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">The &quot;Normal Template&quot; is a file that contains default styles and customizations that determine the basic look of a document, and even active content such as macros.</p><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">In older versions of Word, Microsoft used a binary format (Word 2003 and below), and in Word 2007, Microsoft changed its format to an XML based format, hence the different extensions .dot/.dotx/.dotm.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">The .dotm extension signifies that the &quot;Normal Template&quot; is a macro-enabled template which will come in handy later in this article ;).</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"></p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">The &quot;Normal Template&quot; is similar to other template files, aside from it being the default built-in template of Word, and some features which are not available in ordinary non-default templates.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"></p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">Word cannot open documents without a template, nor can it create new ones without it. Which is why Word has a built-in &quot;Normal template&quot; that would be re-created if Word can&#x27;t find a template to use, or if the current template is corrupted/malformatted.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><h4 id="viewer-76gbu" class="text-base font-semibold group relative grid w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="grid grid-area-1-1 relative -ml-6 w-7 border-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-[0] group-focus:opacity-[0] md:group-hover:md:opacity-[1] md:group-focus:md:opacity-[1] [margin-top:_0.5em]"><a href="#viewer-76gbu" aria-label="Direct link to heading" class="inline-flex h-full items-start dark:text-light/3 dark:shadow-none dark:ring-0 leading-snug"><svg style="mask-image:url(https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v6.6.0/svgs/regular/hashtag.svg?v=2&amp;token=a463935e93);mask-repeat:no-repeat;mask-position:center" class="gb-icon w-3.5 h-[1lh] transition-colors text-transparent group-hover:text-dark/6 dark:group-hover:text-light/5 lg:w-4"></svg></a></div><div class="grid-area-1-1 z-[1] [margin-top:_0.5em]"><strong class="font-bold">Locations:</strong></div></h4><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">The default &quot;Normal Template&quot; is most commonly found in the <strong class="font-bold">User Templates folde</strong>r which is located at:</p><!--/$--><!--$--><ul class="list-none space-y-2 [&amp;&gt;li]:relative [&amp;&gt;li]:ps-[2.25ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;div_div]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-dark/6 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:absolute [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:left-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:w-[1ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:h-[1lh] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:[mask-repeat:no-repeat] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:[mask-position:left] dark:[&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-light/6 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circleFilled [&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circle [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-dash [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-squareFilled [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-square [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circleFilled w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash"><i class="font-italic">%appdata%\Microsoft\Templates\</i></p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--></ul><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">However, this is not the only place Word searches for the &quot;Normal Template&quot;. I examined Word&#x27;s activity when executed and I found two locations that Word searches for the templates, one is Word&#x27;s program folder, the other is the default location for the &quot;Normal Template&quot;.</p><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:0"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 overflow-hidden relative grid dark:ring-light/1 rounded-md h-full aspect-video [max-width:calc(48rem-1px)]"><div class="w-full bg-dark-4/4 dark:bg-light-3/1 grid grid-area-1-1 overflow-hidden [mask:conic-gradient(from_90deg_at_1px_1px,_#0000_90deg,_#0003_0)_calc(50%+1px)_calc(0%+47px)_/_96px_96px]"><div class="aspect-square from-dark-4 to-transparent grid-area-1-1 relative origin-[50%_50%] top-[50%] self-stretch bg-transparent will-change-transform animate-[rotateLoop_2s_linear_infinite] [background-image:conic-gradient(from_-90deg_at_50%_50%,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_0deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_90deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_280deg)] dark:from-light-4/6"></div></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">I did some googling and found an amazingly <a class="underline underline-offset-2 text-primary hover:text-primary-700 transition-colors " href="http://www.wordarticles.com/Articles/Templates/Normal.php">in-depth article by Tony Jollans</a>, Microsoft Word MVP, which mentioned another location that Word is searching for which is actually a registry value that point to a network-shared template.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"></p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">Below is the a list of the templates possible location and their corresponding search order.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><ol class="space-y-2 flex flex-col [&amp;&gt;li]:gap-[1ch] [counter-reset:list-decimal] [&amp;&gt;li]:flex [&amp;&gt;li]:flex-row w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><!--$--><li value="1" class="leading-normal"><div data-value="1" class="bullet ListItem_olListItemBullet__9X19L text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex-1 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl leading-normal min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">Word Program location</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li value="2" class="leading-normal"><div data-value="2" class="bullet ListItem_olListItemBullet__9X19L text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex-1 value="3" class="leading-normal"><div data-value="3" class="bullet ListItem_olListItemBullet__9X19L text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex-1 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto data-value="4" class="bullet ListItem_olListItemBullet__9X19L text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex-1 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl leading-normal min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">GlobalDotName Registry key*</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--></ol><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">*Will be detailed further down this article.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><h4 id="viewer-74njt" class="text-base font-semibold group relative grid w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="grid grid-area-1-1 relative -ml-6 w-7 border-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-[0] group-focus:opacity-[0] md:group-hover:md:opacity-[1] md:group-focus:md:opacity-[1] [margin-top:_0.5em]"><a href="#viewer-74njt" aria-label="Direct link to heading" class="inline-flex h-full items-start dark:text-light/3 dark:shadow-none dark:ring-0 leading-snug"><svg style="mask-image:url(https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v6.6.0/svgs/regular/hashtag.svg?v=2&amp;token=a463935e93);mask-repeat:no-repeat;mask-position:center" class="gb-icon w-3.5 h-[1lh] transition-colors text-transparent group-hover:text-dark/6 dark:group-hover:text-light/5 lg:w-4"></svg></a></div><div class="grid-area-1-1 z-[1] [margin-top:_0.5em]"><strong class="font-bold">Word Program location</strong></div></h4><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">Word searches for the &quot;Normal Template&quot; in Word&#x27;s Program folder which differs on different operating systems versions as well as Microsoft Office versions, you may find it in the following locations:</p><!--/$--><!--$--><ul class="list-none space-y-2 [&amp;&gt;li]:relative [&amp;&gt;li]:ps-[2.25ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;div_div]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-dark/6 number&gt;</i></p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--></ul><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">You can find out Word&#x27;s Program path by its GUI page-api-block:ml-0">The &quot;Normal Template&quot; is rarely located at Word&#x27;s program location,still, you should be aware of this location.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><h4 id="viewer-a3t7u" class="text-base font-semibold group relative grid w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="grid grid-area-1-1 relative -ml-6 w-7 border-0 opacity-0 page-api-block:ml-0"><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">Word uses a default template called Normal.dot / Normal.dotm which can be found in a variety of locations and is loaded with each document&#x27;s execution.</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto document.</strong></p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--></ul><!--/$--><!--$--><h4 id="viewer-ejikn" class="text-base font-semibold group relative grid w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl dark:from-light-4/6"></div></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><strong class="font-bold">How to set it up?</strong></p><!--/$--><!--$--><ol class="space-y-2 flex flex-col [&amp;&gt;li]:gap-[1ch] [counter-reset:list-decimal] [&amp;&gt;li]:flex [&amp;&gt;li]:flex-row [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:tabular-nums [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:whitespace-nowrap [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:list-decimal [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:h-[1lh] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:leading-[inherit] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:flex [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:text-dark/6 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;div_div]:mt-0 dark:[&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:text-light/6 w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><!--$--><li value="1" class="leading-normal"><div data-value="1" class="bullet ListItem_olListItemBullet__9X19L text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex-1 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl leading-normal min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">Create the Value of &quot;GlobalDotName&quot; in the relevant key</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li value="2" class="leading-normal"><div data-value="2" class="bullet ListItem_olListItemBullet__9X19L text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex-1 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl leading-normal min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">In the value&#x27;s data input your path+filename+extension(optional)</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--></ol><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><strong class="font-bold">GlobalDotName Highlights:</strong></p><!--/$--><!--$--><ul class="list-none space-y-2 [&amp;&gt;li]:relative [&amp;&gt;li]:ps-[2.25ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;div_div]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-dark/6 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:absolute [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:left-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:w-[1ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:h-[1lh] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:[mask-repeat:no-repeat] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:[mask-position:left] dark:[&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-light/6 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circleFilled [&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circle [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-dash [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-squareFilled [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-square [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circleFilled w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash"><strong class="font-bold">Takes priority over every other Normal template</strong></p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">Use any location you want</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">Use almost any name/extension you want, they don&#x27;t have to mean anything, yes, even the extension can be total nonsense. DO NOT however choose any meaningful extension to Word aside from the macro-enabled template(.dotm) which is not to be confused with the macro-enabled document(.docm)</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">Well, you actually don&#x27;t even have to choose an extension, it&#x27;ll work anyway without it</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">you can use a relative paths</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">you can also use environment variables by using a REG_EXPAND_SZ Value</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--></ul><!--/$--><!--$--><h3 id="viewer-fr6tk" class="text-2xl font-semibold group relative grid w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="grid grid-area-1-1 relative -ml-6 w-7 border-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-[0] group-focus:opacity-[0] md:group-hover:md:opacity-[1] md:group-focus:md:opacity-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><a href="#viewer-fr6tk" aria-label="Direct link to heading" class="inline-flex h-full items-start dark:text-light/3 dark:shadow-none dark:ring-0 leading-snug"><svg style="mask-image:url(https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v6.6.0/svgs/regular/hashtag.svg?v=2&amp;token=a463935e93);mask-repeat:no-repeat;mask-position:center" class="gb-icon w-3.5 h-[1lh] transition-colors text-transparent group-hover:text-dark/6 dark:group-hover:text-light/5 lg:w-4"></svg></a></div><div class="grid-area-1-1 z-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><strong class="font-bold">Arming a template file with VBA</strong></div></h3><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">1. Open a new document in Word.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">2. Add the &quot;Developer&quot; tab, File -&gt; Options:</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">
</p><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:2"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 overflow-hidden relative grid dark:ring-light/1 rounded-md h-full aspect-video [max-width:calc(48rem-1px)]"><div class="w-full bg-dark-4/4 dark:bg-light-3/1 grid grid-area-1-1 overflow-hidden [mask:conic-gradient(from_90deg_at_1px_1px,_#0000_90deg,_#0003_0)_calc(50%+1px)_calc(0%+47px)_/_96px_96px]"><div class="aspect-square from-dark-4 to-transparent grid-area-1-1 relative origin-[50%_50%] top-[50%] self-stretch bg-transparent will-change-transform animate-[rotateLoop_2s_linear_infinite] [background-image:conic-gradient(from_-90deg_at_50%_50%,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_0deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_90deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_280deg)] dark:from-light-4/6"></div></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">3. Make sure to create your macro in the current document:</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">
</p><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:3"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 overflow-hidden relative grid dark:ring-light/1 rounded-md h-full aspect-video [max-width:calc(48rem-1px)]"><div class="w-full bg-dark-4/4 dark:bg-light-3/1 grid grid-area-1-1 overflow-hidden [mask:conic-gradient(from_90deg_at_1px_1px,_#0000_90deg,_#0003_0)_calc(50%+1px)_calc(0%+47px)_/_96px_96px]"><div class="aspect-square from-dark-4 to-transparent grid-area-1-1 relative origin-[50%_50%] top-[50%] self-stretch bg-transparent will-change-transform animate-[rotateLoop_2s_linear_infinite] [background-image:conic-gradient(from_-90deg_at_50%_50%,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_0deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_90deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_280deg)] dark:from-light-4/6"></div></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:4"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 overflow-hidden relative grid dark:ring-light/1 rounded-md h-full aspect-video [max-width:calc(48rem-1px)]"><div class="w-full bg-dark-4/4 dark:bg-light-3/1 grid grid-area-1-1 overflow-hidden [mask:conic-gradient(from_90deg_at_1px_1px,_#0000_90deg,_#0003_0)_calc(50%+1px)_calc(0%+47px)_/_96px_96px]"><div class="aspect-square from-dark-4 to-transparent grid-area-1-1 relative origin-[50%_50%] top-[50%] self-stretch bg-transparent will-change-transform animate-[rotateLoop_2s_linear_infinite] [background-image:conic-gradient(from_-90deg_at_50%_50%,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_0deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_90deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_280deg)] dark:from-light-4/6"></div></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">This macro will pop a message box</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">4. Once you write your macro, save the document as Normal.dotm (since we are not using GlobalDotName here):</p><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:5"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 overflow-hidden relative grid dark:ring-light/1 rounded-md h-full aspect-video [max-width:calc(48rem-1px)]"><div class="w-full bg-dark-4/4 dark:bg-light-3/1 grid grid-area-1-1 overflow-hidden [mask:conic-gradient(from_90deg_at_1px_1px,_#0000_90deg,_#0003_0)_calc(50%+1px)_calc(0%+47px)_/_96px_96px]"><div class="aspect-square from-dark-4 to-transparent grid-area-1-1 relative origin-[50%_50%] top-[50%] self-stretch bg-transparent will-change-transform animate-[rotateLoop_2s_linear_infinite] [background-image:conic-gradient(from_-90deg_at_50%_50%,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_0deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_90deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_280deg)] dark:from-light-4/6"></div></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:6"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 overflow-hidden relative grid dark:ring-light/1 rounded-md h-full aspect-video [max-width:calc(48rem-1px)]"><div class="w-full bg-dark-4/4 dark:bg-light-3/1 grid grid-area-1-1 overflow-hidden [mask:conic-gradient(from_90deg_at_1px_1px,_#0000_90deg,_#0003_0)_calc(50%+1px)_calc(0%+47px)_/_96px_96px]"><div class="aspect-square from-dark-4 to-transparent grid-area-1-1 relative origin-[50%_50%] top-[50%] self-stretch bg-transparent will-change-transform animate-[rotateLoop_2s_linear_infinite] [background-image:conic-gradient(from_-90deg_at_50%_50%,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_0deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_90deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_280deg)] dark:from-light-4/6"></div></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">5. Now before we implement the GlobalDotName Key and additional important steps(such as setting Trust for our template), lets drop it in the User Template Folder and execute <strong class="font-bold">test.docx, </strong>which is a normal macro-free document.</p><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:7"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 overflow-hidden relative grid dark:ring-light/1 rounded-md h-full aspect-video [max-width:calc(48rem-1px)]"><div class="w-full bg-dark-4/4 dark:bg-light-3/1 grid grid-area-1-1 overflow-hidden [mask:conic-gradient(from_90deg_at_1px_1px,_#0000_90deg,_#0003_0)_calc(50%+1px)_calc(0%+47px)_/_96px_96px]"><div class="aspect-square from-dark-4 to-transparent grid-area-1-1 relative origin-[50%_50%] top-[50%] self-stretch bg-transparent will-change-transform animate-[rotateLoop_2s_linear_infinite] [background-image:conic-gradient(from_-90deg_at_50%_50%,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_0deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_90deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_280deg)] dark:from-light-4/6"></div></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">Modified Normal Template</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">6. And there we have it, a .docx document is opened and executes the macro from the template we just planted.
</p><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:8"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 overflow-hidden relative grid dark:ring-light/1 rounded-md h-full aspect-video [max-width:calc(48rem-1px)]"><div class="w-full bg-dark-4/4 dark:bg-light-3/1 grid grid-area-1-1 overflow-hidden [mask:conic-gradient(from_90deg_at_1px_1px,_#0000_90deg,_#0003_0)_calc(50%+1px)_calc(0%+47px)_/_96px_96px]"><div class="aspect-square from-dark-4 to-transparent grid-area-1-1 relative origin-[50%_50%] top-[50%] self-stretch bg-transparent will-change-transform animate-[rotateLoop_2s_linear_infinite] [background-image:conic-gradient(from_-90deg_at_50%_50%,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_0deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_90deg,_var(--tw-gradient-stops)_280deg)] dark:from-light-4/6"></div></div></div></div><!--/$--><!--$--><h3 id="viewer-eqedi" class="text-2xl font-semibold group relative grid w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="grid grid-area-1-1 relative -ml-6 w-7 border-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-[0] group-focus:opacity-[0] md:group-hover:md:opacity-[1] md:group-focus:md:opacity-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><a href="#viewer-eqedi" aria-label="Direct link to heading" class="inline-flex h-full items-start dark:text-light/3 dark:shadow-none dark:ring-0 leading-snug"><svg style="mask-image:url(https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v6.6.0/svgs/regular/hashtag.svg?v=2&amp;token=a463935e93);mask-repeat:no-repeat;mask-position:center" class="gb-icon w-3.5 h-[1lh] transition-colors text-transparent group-hover:text-dark/6 dark:group-hover:text-light/5 lg:w-4"></svg></a></div><div class="grid-area-1-1 z-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><strong class="font-bold">Trust</strong></div></h3><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">Beginning with Word 2007 and above Microsoft introduced a concept of &quot;Trust&quot; to improve its security and protect its users from unauthorized code running without their knowledge.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">To be able to execute macro without the security warning popping out , you need to either disable the &quot;VBAWarning&quot; value in the registry, or you can add &quot;Trust&quot; to the relevant document by registering it in as &quot;Trusted Document&quot; or place it in a &quot;Trusted location&quot;.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">Luckily, we can control all of these options by editing some registry keys &amp; values. Here are the relevant keys &amp; values locations:</p><!--/$--><!--$--><ul class="list-none space-y-2 [&amp;&gt;li]:relative [&amp;&gt;li]:ps-[2.25ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;div_div]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-dark/6 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:absolute [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:left-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:w-[1ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:h-[1lh] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:[mask-repeat:no-repeat] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:[mask-position:left] dark:[&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-light/6 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circleFilled [&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circle [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-dash [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-squareFilled [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-square [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circleFilled w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Word\Security</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Word\Security\VBAWarning</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Word\Security\Trusted Documents</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Word\Security\Trusted Locations</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Word\Security\Trusted Locations\&lt;key_name_of_location&gt;\</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Word\Security\Trusted Locations\&lt;key_name_of_location&gt;\Path</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Word\Security\Trusted Locations\&lt;key_name_of_location&gt;\AllowSubFolders</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--></ul><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">In this case I will utilize the &quot;Trusted Locations&quot; key to set Trust for a certain location, which means the &quot;VBAWarning&quot; value and the &quot;Trusted Documents&quot; key are not needed for this proof of concept.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><h3 id="viewer-4aqju" class="text-2xl font-semibold group relative grid w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="grid grid-area-1-1 relative -ml-6 w-7 border-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-[0] group-focus:opacity-[0] md:group-hover:md:opacity-[1] md:group-focus:md:opacity-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><a href="#viewer-4aqju" aria-label="Direct link to heading" class="inline-flex h-full items-start dark:text-light/3 dark:shadow-none dark:ring-0 leading-snug"><svg style="mask-image:url(https://ka-p.fontawesome.com/releases/v6.6.0/svgs/regular/hashtag.svg?v=2&amp;token=a463935e93);mask-repeat:no-repeat;mask-position:center" class="gb-icon w-3.5 h-[1lh] transition-colors text-transparent group-hover:text-dark/6 dark:group-hover:text-light/5 lg:w-4"></svg></a></div><div class="grid-area-1-1 z-[1] [margin-top:_0.75em]"><strong class="font-bold">Setting up the persistence</strong></div></h3><!--/$--><!--$--><ul class="list-none space-y-2 [&amp;&gt;li]:relative [&amp;&gt;li]:ps-[2.25ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;div_div]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-dark/6 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:absolute [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:left-0 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:w-[1ch] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:h-[1lh] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:[mask-repeat:no-repeat] [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:[mask-position:left] dark:[&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet]:before:bg-light/6 [&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circleFilled [&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circle [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-dash [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-squareFilled [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-square [&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;_&amp;&gt;li&gt;.bullet:before]:bullet-circleFilled w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><!--$--><li class="leading-normal"><div class="bullet text-base"></div><div class="space-y-2 flex flex-col"><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl min-h-[1lh] flip-heading-hash">Open Word, create a new document, insert your macro to it and save it as a macro-enabled template file (.dotm) in the location you would point GlobalDotName to.</p><!--/$--></div></li><!--/$--></ul><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:9"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 overflow-hidden relative grid </p><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:e"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0"><div class="ring-1 ring-dark/2 [margin-top:_0.75em]">Warning!</div></h3><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">You must create the &quot;Trusted Location&quot; key and place the relevant path value to the template&#x27;s location before any document is executed. Otherwise the document execution will result in an error and the deletion of the crafted template. after the deletion, Word will re-create the &quot;Normal template&quot; from its defaults and place it in the location which GlobalDotName points to.</p><!--/$--><!--$?--><template id="B:10"></template><div role="status" aria-busy="true" class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl Wild</strong></div></h3><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">The usage of templates as means of persistence is leveraged by multiple threat actors and has been spotted in the wild before.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">Having said that, I have yet to encounter the usage of the GlobalDotName which provides a somewhat stealthier implementation of this technique.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto decoration-primary/6 max-w-3xl page-api-block:ml-0">I highly recommend visiting the technique page on <a class="underline underline-offset-2 text-primary hover:text-primary-700 transition-colors " href="https://attack.mitre.org/techniques/T1137/">MITRE ATT&amp;CK </a>which documents some of the threat actors that leverages this technique in-addition to links for various reports that presents its usage.</p><!--/$--><!--$--><p class="w-full mx-auto
